<section class="section-goldilocks section-padding-bottom">

<div class="section-content text-center mb-4">
<h2>Free Online HVAC Quote in Tucson  No Sales Pressure. <span class="d-lg-block">Just Real Pricing.</span></h2>
</p></div>
<div class="col-lg-5">
<div class="section-img mb-3 mb-lg-0">
          <img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" class="border-radiusfull-10 alignnone" src="https://www.idesignac.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/no-sales-pressure.jpg" alt="Free Online HVAC Quote Tucson" width="700" height="500" />
        </div>
</p></div>
<div class="col-lg-7">
<div class="section-Content">
<p>Tucson homeowners: now you can get a <strong>free, accurate HVAC system quote in under 2 minutes</strong>right from your phone or computer. No pushy sales reps. No uncomfortable calls. Just smart, transparent pricing from Southern Arizonas <strong>#1-rated HVAC company</strong>.</p>
<p>At Intelligent Design, we believe homeowners should feel empowered and informed before making big decisions. Thats why weve integrated our <strong>Breakthrough Quote Tool</strong> to deliver <strong>real pricing</strong> based on your needs, your home, and your goals.</p>
</p></div>
</p></div>
</p></div>
<div class="row flex-lg-row flex-column-reverse">
<div class="col-lg-8">
<div class="section-Content">
<h3>Why Use Our Online HVAC Quote Tool?</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Instant Results:</strong> Get a full HVAC system quote in under 2 minutes.</li>
<li><strong>Tailored to Your Home:</strong> Input basic info and get a system matched to your size and comfort goals.</li>
<li><strong>Transparent Pricing:</strong> See detailed estimates with no hidden fees.</li>
<li><strong>Zero Sales Pressure:</strong> We only follow up if you ask us to. No hard closes. Just helpful info.</li>
<li><strong>22,000+ 5-Star Reviews:</strong> Youre working with Tucsons most trusted HVAC team.</li>
</ul>
<p>This quote is more than a numberits your first step toward a cooler, more efficient home.</p>

        </div>

<ul class="d-md-flex green-list-icon two-column-list text-start">

</ul>
<p>All pricing is based on <strong>real installation data</strong> from Southern Arizona homes. If you decide to move forward, our team can perform a free in-home walkthrough to confirm your exact quote.</p>
</p></div>
<div class="section-content">
<h3 class="text-center text-white mb-0">We Make HVAC Simple, Smart, and Local</h3>
<p>Intelligent Design isnt a fly-by-night HVAC company. Weve been Tucsons leading comfort experts for over a decade. All of our installs are done <strong>in-house</strong>no subcontractors, ever.</p>
<p>Were <strong>veteran-owned</strong>, <strong>family-operated</strong>, and we hold an <strong>A+ rating with the BBB</strong>. Every system comes with <strong>industry-leading warranties</strong> and is installed by certified pros who care about your comfort, not your credit card.</p>

<li>Your AC is 10+ years old</li>

<li>Your home doesnt cool evenly</li>

<p>If you checked even one of these boxes, a new system could <strong>pay for itself in comfort and energy savings</strong>and our online quote tool can help you see how.</p>

  function _loadHatchScripts(src) {
    try {
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.src = src;
      script.async = true;
      script.defer = true;
      script.dataset.hatchid = "67f38a719fd92e00011a4e43"; // Replace with your real Hatch ID
      document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0].parentNode.insertBefore(script, null);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Hatch load error:", err);
    }
  }

  window.hatchChatConfig = {
    autoOpen: false
  };

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    _loadHatchScripts("https://hatch-javascript.s3.amazonaws.com/hatchChat-app.js");

    // Repeatedly check if hatch-chat is ready and bind click handlers when it is
    const initChatTriggers = () => {
      const hatchEl = document.querySelector("hatch-chat");

      if (hatchEl && hatchEl.shadowRoot) {
        // Hatch is ready: attach click events to all trigger buttons
        const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#customChatTrigger");
        buttons.forEach(btn => {
          btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
            const openBtn = hatchEl.shadowRoot.querySelector("button#close-pre-engagement");
            if (openBtn) {
              openBtn.click();
            } else {
              console.warn("Open button not found in shadowRoot");
            }
          });
        });
        return; // Stop trying once set
      }

      // Retry every 500ms
      setTimeout(initChatTriggers, 500);
    };

    initChatTriggers();
  });
